      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 17th century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 1700 to 1601 BC there were 230
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 75 were partial, 71 were annular (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 60 were total, and 24 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was five, in 1676 BC, and one month, July 1611 BC, had two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
